			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Operating ratio of 64.1 percent, up 0.6 points.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:6pt 0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:6pt 0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Omaha, Neb., </font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">July</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;"> 23, 2015 </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">&#x2013;</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Union Pacific Corporation (NYSE: UNP) today reported 2015 second quarter net income of $1.2 billion, or $1.38 per diluted share, compared to $1.3 billion, or $1.43 per diluted share, in the second quarter 2014.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:6pt 0pt;line-height:150%;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Solid core pricing gains were not enough to overcome a significant decrease in demand,&#x201D; said Lance Fritz, Union Pacific president and chief executive officer.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#x201C;Total volumes in the second quarter were down 6 percent, led by a sharp decline in coal. Industrial </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">products </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">and agricultural products also posted significant volume decreases.&nbsp;&nbsp;However, we made meaningful progress right sizing our resources to current volumes, and I am </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">encouraged</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;"> to report that we made these improvements while posting </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">strong</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;"> safety performance.&#x201D;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:8pt 0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 10pt">
			&nbsp;
		</p></div><div style="margin-left:72pt;margin-right:72pt;">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">-</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;">-</font>

		</p>

</div>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;;font-size: 12pt"><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;">Second Quarter Summary</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Arial;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 36pt 0pt 0pt;"></font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;">Operating revenue of $5.4 billion was down 10 percent in the second quarter 2015 versus the second quarter 2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;Second quarter business volumes, as measured by total revenue carloads, declined 6 percent compared to 2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;Volume declines in coal, industrial products, and agricultural products more than offset the growth in automotive and intermodal.&nbsp;&nbsp;Chemicals volume was flat </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;">compared to</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;"> 2014 as growth in base chemicals carloads offset a decline in crude oil shipments.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition:</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:150%;font-size:12pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Quarterly freight revenue decreased 10 percent compared to the second quarter 2014, as the volume decline, lower fuel surcharge revenue, and negative business mix more than offset core pricing gains.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:150%;font-size:12pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Union Pacific&#x2019;s 64.1 percent operating ratio was 0.6 points worse than the second quarter 2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;The operating ratio benefited just under a point from the net impact of lower fuel prices in the quarter.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:150%;font-size:12pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Other income of $142 million increased $120 million compared to the second quarter 2014. Included in this amount is the previously announced Fremont, California, land sale, which contributed $113 million to pre-tax income, or 8 cents per </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">diluted </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">share to total earnings.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:150%;font-size:12pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">The $1.99 per gallon average quarterly diesel fuel price in the second quarter 2015 was 36 percent </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">lower than</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;"> the second quarter 2014.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="line-height:150%;color:#000000;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:150%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:150%;color:#000000;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Quarterly train speed, as reported to the Association of American Railroads, was 24.6 mph, about 3 percent faster compared with the second quarter 2014.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt; display: inline;">
			<p style="line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt;margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:150%;font-size:12pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">2015 Outlook</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;line-height:150%;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">&#x201C;While the volume outlook remains uncertain, we </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">remain</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;"> laser focused on operating safely and efficiently no matter what the market environment.&nbsp;&nbsp;We will </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">continue to </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">reduce costs and improve productivity as we </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">further </font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">align resources with demand,&#x201D; Fritz said.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#x201C;Longer term, we continue to be optimistic about the strengths of our diverse rail franchise.&#x201D;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 8pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 1pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-size:1pt;color:#000000;"></font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:6pt 0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">A</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">BOUT UNION PACIFIC</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:6pt 0pt 12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Union Pacific Railroad is the principal operating company of Union Pacific Corporation (NYSE: UNP). One of America's most recognized companies, Union Pacific Railroad connects 23 states in the western two-thirds of the country by rail, providing a critical link in the global supply chain. From 2005-2014, Union Pacific invested more than $31 billion in its network and operations to support America&#x2019;s transportation infrastructure.&nbsp;&nbsp;The railroad&#x2019;s diversified business mix includes Agricultural Products, Automotive, Chemicals, Coal, Industrial Products and Intermodal. Union Pacific&nbsp;&nbsp;serves many of the fastest-growing U.S. population centers, operates from all major West Coast and Gulf Coast ports to eastern gateways, connects with Canada's rail systems and is the only railroad serving all six major Mexico gateways. Union Pacific provides value to its roughly 10,000 customers by delivering products in a safe, reliable, fuel-efficient and environmentally responsible manner.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Union Pacific Investor contact</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">: Mike Staffenbeal at 402-544-4227.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 6pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Arial;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">Union Pacific Media contact</font><font style="display: inline;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">: Aaron Hunt at 402-544-0100.</font>
		</p>
